country_event = {
	id = kirin.1
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event kirin.1"}
	title = kirin.1.t
	desc = kirin.1.d
	
	picture = GFX_event_KIR_evening
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = kirin.1.a
		add_political_power = 70
		set_country_flag = KIR_pol_1_available
		add_ideas =  KIR_pol_1
	}
}

		custom_effect_tooltip = KIR_silence_stability1_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			subtract_from_variable = { var = KIR_plenum_stab_var value = 0.01 }
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = KIR_modify_plenum_communist1_tt
		custom_effect_tooltip = KIR_shuffle_pol_advisors_tt
		custom_effect_tooltip = available_political_advisor

		set_country_flag = KIR_pol_4_available
		hidden_effect = {
			add_to_variable = { var = KIR_plenum_communism_var value = 0.5 }
			set_country_flag = KIR_pol_1_removable
			set_country_flag = KIR_pol_2_removable
			set_country_flag = KIR_pol_3_removable
			set_country_flag = KIR_pol_4_removable
		}
		set_country_flag = KIR_did_not_expel_communists
	}
	
	option = {
		name = kirin.10.b
		add_stability = -0.05
		custom_effect_tooltip = KIR_unlock_entry_autumn_blaze
		add_to_variable = { KIR_diary_SG_protag_1_button_var = 1 }
		meta_effect = {
		  text = {
			set_variable = { KIR_diary_SG_protag_1_entry_[IDKIRX]_var = 3 }
			set_variable = { KIRDiary1Entry[IDKIRX]TitleVar = 3 }
		  }
		  IDKIRX = "[?KIR_diary_SG_protag_1_button_var|0]"
		}
		KIR_unlock_entry_effect = yes
		KIR_diary_SG_protag_1_button_click_effect = yes
		set_country_flag = KIR_expelled_communists
	}
}

					}
				}

				every_controlled_state = {

							state = 926

				country_event = { id = kirin.104 hours = 36 }
				set_variable = { KIR_army_strength_var = KIR.num_battalions } ##determining strength of KIR army
				add_to_variable = { KIR_army_strength_var = 80 } ##strength will be swelled by twenty divisions of four battalions each

				KIC = {

					set_country_flag = KIR_bipartite_war_started_flag

					set_country_flag = KIR_bipartite_war_started_flag 
					set_country_flag = KIR_can_have_banner_system
					set_country_flag = KIR_can_remove_banner_system
					KIR_civil_war_transfer_diary_variables_effect = yes
					set_variable = { var = KIR_develop_1059_decision_cost_var value = 50 }
				}
				set_country_flag = KIR_bipartite_war_started_flag
					set_country_flag = KIR_can_have_banner_system
					set_country_flag = KIR_can_remove_banner_system
				
				set_variable = { KIR_preCW_fascism_popularity_var = party_popularity@fascism }
				set_variable = { KIR_preCW_communism_popularity_var = party_popularity@communism }

				set_variable = { KIR_preCW_neutrality_popularity_var = party_popularity@neutrality }

				clr_country_flag = KIR_pol_4_available

				retire_ideology_leader = communism
			}

		else_if = {

			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = neutrality
				popularity = 0.05
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = kirin_loyalists.13.b
		add_political_power = 25
	}
}

		hidden_effect = {
			clr_country_flag = KIR_power_struggle_ongoing_flag
			remove_ideas = KIR_power_struggle_WF_60_hidden_buffs
			remove_ideas = KIR_power_struggle_RS_60_hidden_buffs
			remove_ideas = KIR_power_struggle_WF_75_hidden_buffs
			remove_ideas = KIR_power_struggle_RS_75_hidden_buffs
			clear_variable = KIR_power_struggle_WF_var
			clear_variable = KIR_power_struggle_RS_var
			remove_mission = KIR_power_struggle_death_spiral_WF_mission
			remove_mission = KIR_power_struggle_death_spiral_RS_mission
		}
	}
	title = kirin_loyalists.27.t
	desc = kirin_loyalists.27.d
	
	picture = GFX_event_KIR_evening
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	trigger = {
		original_tag = KIR
		KIR = {
			exists = yes
			has_country_flag = KIR_bipartite_war_started_flag
			has_country_flag = KIR_power_struggle_ongoing_flag
			has_country_flag = KIS_council_salvation_front_civil_war_scenario
			NOT = {
				has_completed_focus = KIR_civil_war_focus_7e
				has_completed_focus = KIR_civil_war_focus_7x
			}
			KIS = {
				NOT = {
					has_war_with = KIR
				}
				OR = {
					exists = no
					is_subject_of = ROOT
					has_capitulated = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = kirin_loyalists.27.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = KIR_civil_war_power_struggle_ends_tt
		custom_effect_tooltip = KIR_civil_war_PS_compromise_tt
		set_country_flag = KIR_civil_war_PS_compromise_flag
	}
}

			KIS = {
				is_subject_of = KIR
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = kirin_council.34.d_2
		trigger = {
			KIS = {
				NOT = {
					is_subject_of = KIR
				}
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = kirin_council.34.d_3
		trigger = {
			KIR = {
				is_subject_of = KIS
			}
			KIS = {
				has_cosmetic_tag = KIS_KIR
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = kirin_council.34.d_4
		trigger = {
			KIR = {
				is_subject_of = KIS
			}
		}
	}
	
	picture = GFX_event_KIR_evening
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = kirin_council.34.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = fascism
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = fascism
				popularity = 0.15
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = neutrality
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = neutrality
				popularity = 0.15
			}
		}
		KIR_alleviate_civil_war_idea_effect = yes
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = kirin_council.51
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event kirin_council.51"}
	immediate = {
		set_variable = { KIR_loot_cities_1059_civ_level = 1059.industrial_complex_level }
		set_variable = { KIR_loot_cities_1059_mil_level = 1059.arms_factory_level }
		set_variable = { KIR_loot_cities_1073_civ_level = 1073.industrial_complex_level }
		set_variable = { KIR_loot_cities_1073_mil_level = 1073.arms_factory_level }
		set_variable = { KIR_loot_cities_1073_nav_level = 1073.building_level@dockyard }
	}
	title = kirin_council.51.t
	desc = kirin_council.51.d
	
	picture = GFX_event_KIR_evening
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = kirin_council.51.a
		hidden_effect = {
			1059 = {
				remove_building = {
					type = industrial_complex 
					level = KIS.KIR_loot_cities_1059_civ_level
				}
				remove_building = {
					type = arms_factory 
					level = KIS.KIR_loot_cities_1059_mil_level
				}
			}
			1073 = {
				remove_building = {
					type = industrial_complex 
					level = KIS.KIR_loot_cities_1073_civ_level
				}
				remove_building = {
					type = arms_factory 
					level = KIS.KIR_loot_cities_1073_mil_level
				}
				remove_building = {
					type = dockyard 
					level = KIS.KIR_loot_cities_1073_nav_level
				}
			}
			while_loop_effect = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { KIS.KIR_loot_cities_1059_civ_level > 0 }
				}
				random_owned_controlled_state = {
					limit = {
						is_core_of = KIS
					}
					add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
					add_building_construction = {
						type = industrial_complex
						level = 1
						instant_build = yes
					}
				}
				subtract_from_variable = { KIS.KIR_loot_cities_1059_civ_level = 1 }
			}
			while_loop_effect = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { KIS.KIR_loot_cities_1059_mil_level > 0 }
				}
				random_owned_controlled_state = {
					limit = {
						is_core_of = KIS
					}
					add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
					add_building_construction = {
						type = arms_factory
						level = 1
						instant_build = yes
					}
				}
				subtract_from_variable = { KIS.KIR_loot_cities_1059_mil_level = 1 }
			}
			while_loop_effect = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { KIS.KIR_loot_cities_1073_civ_level > 0 }
				}
				random_owned_controlled_state = {
					limit = {
						is_core_of = KIS
					}
					add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
					add_building_construction = {
						type = industrial_complex
						level = 1
						instant_build = yes
					}
				}
				subtract_from_variable = { KIS.KIR_loot_cities_1073_civ_level = 1 }
			}
			while_loop_effect = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { KIS.KIR_loot_cities_1073_mil_level > 0 }
				}
				random_owned_controlled_state = {
					limit = {
						is_core_of = KIS
					}
					add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
					add_building_construction = {
						type = arms_factory
						level = 1
						instant_build = yes
					}
				}
				subtract_from_variable = { KIS.KIR_loot_cities_1073_mil_level = 1 }
			}
			while_loop_effect = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { KIS.KIR_loot_cities_1073_nav_level > 0 }
				}
				random_owned_controlled_state = {
					limit = {
						is_core_of = KIS
						is_coastal = yes
					}
					add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
					add_building_construction = {
						type = dockyard
						level = 1
						instant_build = yes
					}
				}
				subtract_from_variable = { KIS.KIR_loot_cities_1073_nav_level = 1 }
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = KIR_empire_focus_2b_tt
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = kirin_council.69 ##BASED
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event kirin_council.69"}
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			create_dynamic_country = {
				original_tag = KIS
				save_event_target_as = KIS_AUB_ENEZ_target
				set_country_flag = KIS_AUB_ENEZ_flag
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							is_core_of = AUB
							is_core_of = KIS
						}
					}
					remove_core_of = AUB
				}
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = fascism
					elections_allowed = no
				}
				set_popularities = {
					democratic = 0
					neutrality = 0

					communism = 0
				}
				KIS = { 
					AUB = { 
						transfer_technology = yes 
						transfer_society_ideas = yes
						transfer_science_ideas = yes
						transfer_poverty_ideas = yes
						transfer_illiteracy_ideas = yes
					} 
				}
				add_ideas = low_economic_mobilisation
				add_ideas = free_trade
				add_ideas = kirin_race
				add_ideas = limited_conscription
				add_ideas = KIR_pirate_thalassocracy

					ideology = fascism 
					long_name = KIRIN_VERMILION_PARTY_fascism_LONG
					name = KIRIN_VERMILION_PARTY_fascism
				}
				set_cosmetic_tag = KIR_pirate
				set_cosmetic_tag = KIS_AUB_KIR
				load_focus_tree = blank_focus_tree
				set_rule = {
					can_create_factions = no
					can_boost_other_ideologies = no
					can_join_factions = no
					can_send_volunteers = yes
					can_puppet = no
					can_lower_tension = no
				}
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Roaring Fire"
					desc = "KIR_roaring_fire_desc"
					picture = "gfx/leaders/KIR/roaring_fire.tga"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = bandit
					traits = {
					}
				}
				transfer_state = 833
				transfer_state = 1065
				set_capital = 833
				division_template = {
					name = "Private Marine Para-Militia"
					regiments = {
						marine = { x = 0 y = 0 }
						marine = { x = 0 y = 1 }
						marine = { x = 1 y = 0 }
						marine = { x = 1 y = 1 }
						marine = { x = 2 y = 0 }
						marine = { x = 2 y = 1 }
					}
					support = {
						recon = { x = 0 y = 0 }
						artillery = { x = 0 y = 1 }
					}
				}
				833 = {
					add_core_of = PREV
					create_unit = {
						division = "name = \"Marine Para-Militia Onyx-90\" division_template = \"Private Marine Para-Militia\" start_experience_factor = 0.44 start_equipment_factor = 1" 
						owner = PREV
						count = 1
					}
				}
				1065 = {
					add_core_of = PREV
					add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
					add_building_construction = {
						type = dockyard
						level = 1
						instant_build = yes
					}
					create_unit = {
						division = "name = \"Marine Para-Militia Obsidian-91\" division_template = \"Private Marine Para-Militia\" start_experience_factor = 0.5 start_equipment_factor = 1" 
						owner = PREV
						count = 1
					}
					create_unit = {
						division = "name = \"Marine Para-Militia Olive-92\" division_template = \"Private Marine Para-Militia\" start_experience_factor = 0.44 start_equipment_factor = 1" 
						owner = PREV
						count = 1
					}
				}
				reserve_dynamic_country = yes
			}
			puppet = AUB
		}

country_event = {
	id = kirin_council.508
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event kirin_council.508"}
	immediate = {
		set_variable = { KIS_SYCEE_CONTRACT_OFFER = 25000 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { KIS_SYCEE_CONTRACT_OFFER = KIS_GUILD_CONTRACT_OFFER }
			}
			add_to_variable = { KIS_SYCEE_CONTRACT_OFFER = 25000 }
		}
	}
	title = kirin_council.508.t
	desc = kirin_council.508.d
	
	picture = GFX_event_KIR_evening
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		original_tag = KIS
		has_country_flag = KIS_corporate_war_happened_flag
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = KIS_corporate_war_KAG_offer_ACCEPTED_flag
		}
		STH = {
			exists = yes
			KAG = {
				has_war_with = PREV
			}
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 45
	}
	
	option = {
		name = kirin_council.508.a
		unlock_decision_tooltip = KIS_corporate_war_STH_mercs_decision
		set_country_flag = KIS_corporate_war_STH_offer_flag
		custom_effect_tooltip = KIS_corporate_war_STH_mercs_decision_event_tt
	}
}

	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event kirin_council.300"}
	title = kirin_council.300.t
	desc = kirin_council.300.d
	
	picture = GFX_event_KIR_evening
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		original_tag = KIS
		has_country_flag = KIS_unlock_empire_focus_tree
		controls_state = 816
		controls_state = 1069
		controls_state = 1073
		controls_state = 1076
		controls_state = 1077
		controls_state = 1078
		controls_state = 1081
		OR = {
			check_variable = { core_resistance@KIR > 30 }
			check_variable = { core_resistance@KIC > 30 }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = kirin_council.300.a
		add_political_power = -30
		custom_effect_tooltip = KIS_council_300_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			every_controlled_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_core_of = KIR 
						is_core_of = KIC
					}
				}
				add_resistance = 3
			}
		}
	}
}
